              \n                    </span>\n                \n\n                 \n                \n                    \n                \n                        <p>Stone by stone, the Ancestral Puebloans built a sprawling community of architecturally impressive “great houses” in northwestern New Mexico. Pueblo Bonito is the oldest and largest, and it was apparently the center of the Chaco world, a destination for hundreds who traveled there at certain times of the year from distant great houses for vital celebrations or rites. </p>\n                    \n                \n                </div>\n            \n                <div class=\"zebra-stripes\">\n                    <ul
